<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мчаться.html>мча́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mčátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:помянуть.html>помяну́ть</a> (9405)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помянуть.html>помяну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pomjanútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поминать.html>помина́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to remember, to recall</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to mention</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">religion</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pray for the health living or the repose of the soul of the dead, to commemorate</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:помять.html>помя́ть</a> (14946)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мять.html>мять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помять.html>помя́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pomjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мять.html>мять</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rumple, to crumple, to wrinkle, to fumble, to crease</li>
<li>to dent</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to press, to squeeze</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:понадобиться.html>пона́добиться</a> (2031)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на́доба</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nádoba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понадобиться.html>пона́добиться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ponádobitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>no imperfective form is used</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>to need, to be needed, to become necessary
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>Для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понадобиться.html>пона́добится</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:некоторый.html>не́которое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Dlja étovo <b>ponádobitsja</b> nékotoroje vrémja.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">It will take some time.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зачем.html>заче́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понадобиться.html>пона́добилось</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:уезжать.html>уезжа́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:далеко.html>далеко́</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Začém jemú <b>ponádobilosʹ</b> ujezžátʹ tak dalekó?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Why did he need to go so far away?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to come in handy</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to be needed</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потребоваться.html>потре́боваться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">potrébovatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:понаехать.html>понае́хать</a> (22590)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наехать.html>нае́хать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">najéxatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to come in large numbers</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>

***понедельник.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:понедельник.html>понеде́льник</a> (4378)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">понедѣльникъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ponedělĭnikŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ponedělьnikъ</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">after</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">неде́ль-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nedélʹ-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Sunday; week</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, meaning a day after Sunday.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понедельник.html>понеде́льник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ponedélʹnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понедельник.html>понеде́льника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понедельник.html>понеде́льники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понедельник.html>понеде́льников</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Monday
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понедельник.html>понеде́льник</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>ponedélʹnik</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">on Monday</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понедельник.html>понеде́льникам</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po <b>ponedélʹnikam</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">on Mondays</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понедельник.html>понеде́льнику</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">k <b>ponedélʹniku</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">by Monday</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понедельник.html>понеде́льника</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>ponedélʹnika</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">from Monday</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понедельник.html>понеде́льника</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пятница.html>пя́тницы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>ponedélʹnika</b> do pjátnicy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">from Monday to Friday</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:следовать.html>сле́дующий</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понедельник.html>понеде́льник</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v slédujuščij <b>ponedélʹnik</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">next Monday</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***понемногу.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:понемногу.html>понемно́гу</a> (5789)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понемногу.html>понемно́гу</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ponemnógu</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>bit by bit, little by little <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">small amount at a time</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***понестись.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:понестись.html>понести́сь</a> (6971)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понести.html>понести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ponestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-сь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понестись.html>понести́сь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ponestísʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нестись.html>нести́сь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rush off <i>(after)</i>, to dash off <i>(after)</i>, to tear along <i>(after)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понестись.html>понёсся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>ни́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>ponjóssja</b> za ními</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he rushed/dashed off after them; he tore after them</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понести.html>понести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ponestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***понижать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:понижать.html>понижа́ть</a> (17538)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понизить.html>пони́зить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ponízitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понижать.html>понижа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ponižátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понизить.html>пони́зить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lower, to reduce
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:понижать.html>понижа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:цена.html>цены</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ponižátʹ</b> ceny</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lower/reduce prices</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:понижать.html>понижа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:голос.html>го́лос</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ponižátʹ</b> gólos</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lower/drop one's voice</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to demote
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пониженный.html>пони́жен</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:звание.html>зва́нии</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on byl ponížen v zvánii</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he was demoted/lowered in rank</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снижать.html>снижа́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">snižátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уменьшать.html>уменьша́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">umenʹšátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
